				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
				} );
			</script>

<script>
	jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
		if (localStorage.getItem('postView') === 'grid-view-active') {
			$('#post_archive').addClass('grid-view-active');
			$('.post-layout_grid').addClass('active');
		} else if (localStorage.getItem('postView') === 'list-view-active') {
			$('#post_archive').addClass('list-view-active');
			$('.post-layout_list').addClass('active');
		} else {
			$('#post_archive').removeClass('grid-view-active');
			$('#post_archive').removeClass('list-view-active');
		}
		// Grid View
		$('.post-layout_grid').click(function() {
			localStorage.setItem('postView', 'grid-view-active');
			$('#post_archive').addClass('grid-view-active');
			$('#post_archive').removeClass('list-view-active');
			// Grid Button
			$('.post-layout_grid').removeClass('inactive');
			// List Button
			$('.post-layout_list.active').removeClass('active');
			$('.post-layout_list').addClass('inactive');
			$(this).addClass('active');
		});
		// List View
		$('.post-layout_list').click(function() {
			localStorage.setItem('postView', 'list-view-active');
			$('#post_archive').addClass('list-view-active');
			$('#post_archive').removeClass('grid-view-active');
			// Grid Button
			$('.post-layout_grid.active').removeClass('active');
			$('.post-layout_grid').addClass('inactive');
			// List Button
			$('.post-layout_list').removeClass('inactive');
			$(this).addClass('active');
		});
	});
</script>

<script>
var pbjs = pbjs || {};
pbjs.que = pbjs.que || [];

var googletag = googletag || {};
googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];

var headerBiddingSlots = [];

function sendAdServerRequest(slots) {
  if (pbjs.adserverRequestSent) return;
  pbjs.adserverRequestSent = true;
  googletag.cmd.push(function () {
    googletag.pubads().refresh(slots);
  });
}

googletag.cmd.push(function () {
  var mappingLarge = googletag.sizeMapping()
    .addSize([1025,0], [[300,600],[300,250]])
    .addSize([768,0], [[300,250]])
    .addSize([480,0], [[300,250]])
    .addSize([320,0], [[300,250]])
    .build();

  var mappingSmall = googletag.sizeMapping()
    .addSize([768,0], [])
    .addSize([480,0], [[320,50]])
    .addSize([320,0], [[320,50]])
    .build();

  headerBiddingSlots.push(
    googletag.defineSlot('/135062774,22908453228/tvtonight.sections-POS1', [[300,250]], 'div-gpt-ad-sections-POS1')
      .addService(googletag.pubads())
  );

  headerBiddingSlots.push(
    googletag.defineSlot('/135062774,22908453228/tvtonight.sections-POS2', [[300,600],[300,250]], 'div-gpt-ad-sections-POS2')
      .defineSizeMapping(mappingLarge)
      .addService(googletag.pubads())
  );

  var anchorSlot = googletag.defineSlot('/135062774,22908453228/tvtonight.sections-ANCHOR', [[320,50]], 'div-gpt-ad-sections-ANCHOR')
    .defineSizeMapping(mappingSmall)
    .addService(googletag.pubads());
  headerBiddingSlots.push(anchorSlot);

  googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
  googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs();
  googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
  googletag.pubads().enableAsyncRendering();
  googletag.enableServices();

  googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-sections-POS1');
  googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-sections-POS2');
  googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-sections-ANCHOR');

  pbjs.que.push(function () {
    pbjs.rp.requestBids({
      callback: function () { sendAdServerRequest(headerBiddingSlots); },
      gptSlotObjects: headerBiddingSlots
    });

    setTimeout(function () { sendAdServerRequest(headerBiddingSlots); }, 3000);
  });
});
</script>
